SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[AssignedToId], [b].[Complexity], [b].[CreatedAt], [b].[Description], [b].[DueDate], [b].[IsDeleted], [b].[IsMovedToSprint], [b].[Priority], [b].[ProjectId], [b].[SprintId], [b].[Status], [b].[StoryPoints], [b].[Title], [b].[UpdatedAt], [s0].[Id], [s0].[CreatedAt], [s0].[EndDate], [s0].[Goal], [s0].[IsDeleted], [s0].[Name], [s0].[ProjectId], [s0].[StartDate], [s0].[Status], [s0].[UpdatedAt], [s1].[Id], [s1].[BacklogItemId], [s1].[CreatedAt], [s1].[IsDeleted], [s1].[IsDone], [s1].[Title], [s1].[UpdatedAt], [s1].[Id0], [s2].[Id], [s2].[AuthorId], [s2].[AuthorName], [s2].[BacklogItemId], [s2].[Content], [s2].[CreatedAt], [s2].[IsDeleted], [s2].[UpdatedAt], [s2].[Id0]
FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[EndDate], [s].[Goal], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[Name], [s].[ProjectId], [s].[StartDate], [s].[Status], [s].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Sprints] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s0] ON [b].[SprintId] = [s0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[BacklogItemId], [b0].[CreatedAt], [b0].[IsDeleted], [b0].[IsDone], [b0].[Title], [b0].[UpdatedAt], [b2].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [BacklogSubTasks] AS [b0]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b1].[Id], [b1].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b1]
        WHERE [b1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b2] ON [b0].[BacklogItemId] = [b2].[Id]
    WHERE [b2].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s1] ON [b].[Id] = [s1].[BacklogItemId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b3].[Id], [b3].[AuthorId], [b3].[AuthorName], [b3].[BacklogItemId], [b3].[Content], [b3].[CreatedAt], [b3].[IsDeleted], [b3].[UpdatedAt], [b5].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [BacklogComments] AS [b3]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b4].[Id], [b4].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b4]
        WHERE [b4].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b5] ON [b3].[BacklogItemId] = [b5].[Id]
    WHERE [b5].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s2] ON [b].[Id] = [s2].[BacklogItemId]
WHERE [b].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [b].[ProjectId] = @projectId AND [b].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
ORDER BY [b].[Priority], [b].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s1].[Id], [s1].[Id0], [s2].[Id]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[EndDate], [s].[Goal], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[Name], [s].[ProjectId], [s].[StartDate], [s].[Status], [s].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Sprints] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s0] ON [b].[SprintId] = [s0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[BacklogItemId], [b0].[CreatedAt], [b0].[IsDeleted], [b0].[IsDone], [b0].[Title], [b0].[UpdatedAt], [b2].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [BacklogSubTasks] AS [b0]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b1].[Id], [b1].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b1]
        WHERE [b1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b2] ON [b0].[BacklogItemId] = [b2].[Id]
    WHERE [b2].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s1] ON [b].[Id] = [s1].[BacklogItemId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b3].[Id], [b3].[AuthorId], [b3].[AuthorName], [b3].[BacklogItemId], [b3].[Content], [b3].[CreatedAt], [b3].[IsDeleted], [b3].[UpdatedAt], [b5].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [BacklogComments] AS [b3]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b4].[Id], [b4].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b4]
        WHERE [b4].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b5] ON [b3].[BacklogItemId] = [b5].[Id]
    WHERE [b5].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s2] ON [b].[Id] = [s2].[BacklogItemId]
WHERE [b].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [b].[ProjectId] = @projectId AND [b].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
ORDER BY [b].[Priority], [b].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s1].[Id], [s1].[Id0], [s2].[Id]

FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[EndDate], [s].[Goal], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[Name], [s].[ProjectId], [s].[StartDate], [s].[Status], [s].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Sprints] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s0] ON [b].[SprintId] = [s0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[BacklogItemId], [b0].[CreatedAt], [b0].[IsDeleted], [b0].[IsDone], [b0].[Title], [b0].[UpdatedAt], [b2].[Id] AS [Id0]

        SELECT [b1].[Id], [b1].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b1]
        WHERE [b1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b2] ON [b0].[BacklogItemId] = [b2].[Id]
    WHERE [b2].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s1] ON [b].[Id] = [s1].[BacklogItemId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b3].[Id], [b3].[AuthorId], [b3].[AuthorName], [b3].[BacklogItemId], [b3].[Content], [b3].[CreatedAt], [b3].[IsDeleted], [b3].[UpdatedAt], [b5].[Id] AS [Id0]

        SELECT [b4].[Id], [b4].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b4]
        WHERE [b4].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b5] ON [b3].[BacklogItemId] = [b5].[Id]
    WHERE [b5].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s2] ON [b].[Id] = [s2].[BacklogItemId]
WHERE [b].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [b].[ProjectId] = @projectId AND [b].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[EndDate], [s].[Goal], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[Name], [s].[ProjectId], [s].[StartDate], [s].[Status], [s].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Sprints] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s0] ON [b].[SprintId] = [s0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[BacklogItemId], [b0].[CreatedAt], [b0].[IsDeleted], [b0].[IsDone], [b0].[Title], [b0].[UpdatedAt], [b2].[Id] AS [Id0]

        WHERE [b1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b2] ON [b0].[BacklogItemId] = [b2].[Id]
    WHERE [b2].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s1] ON [b].[Id] = [s1].[BacklogItemId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b3].[Id], [b3].[AuthorId], [b3].[AuthorName], [b3].[BacklogItemId], [b3].[Content], [b3].[CreatedAt], [b3].[IsDeleted], [b3].[UpdatedAt], [b5].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [BacklogComments] AS [b3]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b4].[Id], [b4].[IsDeleted]
        FROM [BacklogItems] AS [b4]
        WHERE [b4].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [b5] ON [b3].[BacklogItemId] = [b5].[Id]
    WHERE [b5].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s2] ON [b].[Id] = [s2].[BacklogItemId]
